<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a> (1937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongen.html>tonge</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tunga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tungǭ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dn̥ǵʰwéh₂s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongen.html>tongen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongetje.html>tongetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From etymology 1.
</p>

***tongs.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a> (112163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:tong.html>tong</a> ("tool for manipulating <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> in a fire") + -s
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument or tool used for picking <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> up without touching them with the hands or <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a>, consisting of two slats or <a href = vnd.unilang:grips.html>grips</a> hinged at the end or in the middle, and sometimes including a spring to open the <a href = vnd.unilang:grips.html>grips</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1977</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Agatha_Christie" class="extiw" title="w:Agatha Christie"><a href = vnd.unilang:agatha.html>Agatha</a> Christie</a>,  chapter 4, in  <cite>An Autobiography</cite>, part II, London |  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Collins,_Sons" class="extiw" title="w:William Collins, Sons">Collins</a>, <small>→ISBN</small>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> also hairdressing: hairdressing, too, really <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> hairdressing in those times — no running a comb through it and that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> that. It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> curled, frizzed, waved, put in curlers overnight, waved with hot <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></b>;<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large scissors-like two-piece center-hinged forged-iron implement with oval-loop handles and with pointed <a href = vnd.unilang:tips.html>tips</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> inward (in the same plane as and perpendicular to the handles) to facilitate lifting and carrying a block of ice. Often called ice <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a>.</li></ol>

***tooien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tooien.html>tooien</a> (98625)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōien</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:touwen.html>touwen</a></i> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:touwen.html>touwen</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tawjaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to adorn, decorate</li></ol>

***toom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a> (78911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*tōm</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*taumaz</i>.
Doublet with Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">team</i>, from English.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tomen.html>tomen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bridle, rein
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>Je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> You really need to keep those boys in check</dd></dl></li>
<li>a flock of <a href = vnd.unilang:birds.html>birds</a> (especially ducks, geese and <a href = vnd.unilang:swans.html>swans</a>)</li>
<li>frenulum</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:toom.html>toom</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***toon.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a> (1807)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tonus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toontje.html>toontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>tone</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toontje.html>toontje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Dated form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">teen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The front portion of a hoof.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Still used in some dialects in <a href = vnd.unilang:utrecht.html>Utrecht</a> and Holland in the meaning “toe”. This variant seems to have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> quite common in Hollandic dialects until the 19th century. Similar forms have also <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> found to exist in certain West Frisian and Dutch Low Saxon dialects.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toonaard.html>toonaard</a> (67087)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aard.html>aard</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Tonart</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mode <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">major scale or minor scale</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toonsoort.html>toonsoort</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">torn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*torn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*turnaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zorn</i>.
</p>

***toornig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toornig.html>toornig</a> (112159)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toorn.html>toorn</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ire, wrath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">zornig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toornig.html>toornig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toornig.html>toorniger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">toornigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>outraged, ireful, wrathful</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Bijvoeglijk_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoeglijk.html>Bijvoeglijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***toothpick.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a> (72394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tooth</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pick</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toothpicks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small, usually wooden, stick, often pointed at both <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a>, for removing food residue from between the teeth.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">dentiscalp</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">picktooth</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">toothpicks</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toothpicking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toothpicked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To spear (food) on a <a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To transfer (a sample of bacteria, etc.) by means of a <a href = vnd.unilang:toothpick.html>toothpick</a>.</li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طَاقِيَّة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭāqiyya</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toque_(French)" class="extiw" title="w:Toque (French)"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Toque_(French)" class="extiw" title="w:Toque (French)">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toques</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A type of hat with no brim.
<ul><li><b>1903</b>—Janet Elder Rait, <i>Alison Howard</i>, Archibald Constable amp; Co., page 273,
<dl><dd>"Because Esmé <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> going out this afternoon to choose a new <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>, and she hoped I should like it, and I’m not quite sure what it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, or where she'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> wear it. Do you mind explaining?"</dd>
<dd>"Not at all. A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that which if it <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strings.html>strings</a> would be a bonnet, and if it <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> brim, would be a hat. It <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> worn on the head."</dd>
<dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>Thanks</a>, now I know where I am," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> the vicar of St. Machars, with a sigh of relief.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1932</b>—Vyvyan Holland, translator, <i>The Strange River</i> by <a href = vnd.unilang:julien.html>Julien</a> Green, Harper amp; Brothers, page 180,
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:drank.html>drank</a> a glass of wine mixed with water, <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> off her felt <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> and her <a href = vnd.unilang:shoes.html>shoes</a>, and slid beneath the red eiderdown.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1957</b>—<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Samuel_Beckett" class="extiw" title="w:Samuel Beckett">Samuel Beckett</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Endgame_(play)" class="extiw" title="w:Endgame (play)">"<a href = vnd.unilang:endgame.html>Endgame</a>"</a>,
<dl><dd>In a dressing-gown, a stiff <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> on his head, a large blood-stained handkerchief <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his face, a whistle hanging from his neck, a <a href = vnd.unilang:rug.html>rug</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his knees, thick <a href = vnd.unilang:socks.html>socks</a> on his <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hamm.html>Hamm</a> seems to be asleep.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">specifically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tall white hat with no brim of the sort worn by <a href = vnd.unilang:chefs.html>chefs</a>
<ul><li><b>1999</b>—Michael Ruhlman, <i>The Making of a <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>Chef</a>: Mastering Heat at the Culinary Institute of America</i>, Owl Books, →ISBN, page 154,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>Chef</a> Felder <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> in her early forties, slender, with short wavy brown hair, almost all of which could be contained within her <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2000</b>—Jerrilyn Farmer, <i>Killer Wedding</i>, HarperCollins, →ISBN, page 103,
<dl><dd>When I <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to the back of a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>'s head, wearing a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>, I <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> I'd spotted my quarry.</dd>
<dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>Chef</a> Reynoso?"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2004</b>—Laura Levine, <i>Killer <a href = vnd.unilang:blonde.html>Blonde</a></i>, Kensington Books, →ISBN, page 114,
<dl><dd>Minutes <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a>, a red-faced <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> in a <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>chef</a>'s <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> approached our table.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>chef</a>.
<ul><li><b>2007</b>—October, Nicole Berrie, "Green Eggs and <a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a>", in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Elle" class="extiw" title="w:Elle"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:elle.html>Elle</a></i></a>, page 360,
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> Mason first grabbed the spotlight as the pastry <a href = vnd.unilang:chef.html>chef</a> ... for being the most rock 'n' roll <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b> in town.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A variety of bonnet monkey; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/toque_macaque" class="extiw" title="w:toque macaque"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a> macaque</a>, <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Macaca_sinica" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Macaca sinica"><i>Macaca sinica</i></a></span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An African nominal money of account, equal to 40 cowries.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1871. Assimilated from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canadian_French" class="extiw" title="w:Canadian French">Canadian French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tuque</i>. Likely to be an hypercorrection from the time that <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> already in the dictionaries when they didn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> yet list <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tuque</i> as a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of hat. French word <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tuque</i> for hat <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> itself not strictly a deformation of French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i> : it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also related to other meanings of <i>tuque</i> and to its former name <i>bonnet à la turque</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:lit.html>lit</a>. Turkish-style bunnet/cap).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tuque" class="extiw" title="w:Tuque">Tuque</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tuque" class="extiw" title="w:Tuque">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toques</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A knitted hat, usually conical but of varying shape, often woollen, and sometimes topped by a pom-pom or tassel.
<ul><li><b>1998</b>, Douglas Coupland, <i>Girlfriend in a <a href = vnd.unilang:coma.html>Coma</a></i>, ch 1:
<dl><dd>Such <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the demented nature of the universe that I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> too weak to properly respond to my being hit on by carloads of Betties and Veronicas—all except for the cheeky Cheryl Anderson who <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> ‘manual release’ the day I <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> my eye-brows, followed by a flood of <a href = vnd.unilang:tears.html>tears</a> and the snapping of <a href = vnd.unilang:polaroids.html>Polaroids</a> in which I wear a knit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></b>. Gush gush.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b> March,  <a href = vnd.unilang:laura.html>Laura</a> Bliss,  “How WeWork <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>Has</a> Perfectly Captured the Millennial Id”, in  <cite>The Atlantic</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.theatlantic.com/magazine/archive/2018/03/wework-the-perfect-manifestation-of-the-millennial-id/550922/">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">It <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> like entering the Millennial id. Craft <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> and cucumber water poured from kitchen <a href = vnd.unilang:taps.html>taps</a>. Laptoppers in <a href = vnd.unilang:jeans.html>jeans</a> and <b>toques</b> clacked along to MGMT in the wood-paneled common area.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:beanie.html>beanie</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">knit cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">stocking cap</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">watch cap</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toque.html>toque</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toques</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rhythm used in Latin music, especially Cuban religious rituals.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The guitar part of <a href = vnd.unilang:flamenco.html>flamenco</a> music.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> tor (18261)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b>tor</b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:insecten.html>insecten</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> insect <a href = vnd.unilang:waarvan.html>waarvan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vleugels.html>vleugels</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewoonlijk.html>gewoonlijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schuilgaan.html>schuilgaan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stevige.html>stevige</a> dekbladen (<i>Coleoptera</i>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">torre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">turn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tur</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">turris</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">torpēdō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">numbness, torpidity, electric <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>ray</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">torpeō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I am stiff, numb, torpid; I am astounded; I am inactive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-dō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noun <a href = vnd.unilang:suffix.html>suffix</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ster.html>ster</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stiff</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span ***torsen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:torsen.html>torsen</a> (55751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:torsen.html>torsen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pack, load</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare metathesized <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:trossen.html>trossen</a></i>, meaning the same), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">torser</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pack, bind together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">trousser</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*torsare</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*torsus</i>, a variant form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tortus</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">torqueō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:torsen.html>torsen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To carry or bear with difficulty.</li></ol>

***tosh.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a> (16453)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From 19th-century British <a href = vnd.unilang:thieves.html>thieves</a>' cant, of uncertain origin. Sense of nonsense possibly influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tush</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nonsense! <a href = vnd.unilang:tsk.html>tsk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tsk.html>tsk</a>!</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> attested from 15th century.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Copper; <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a> made of copper
<ul><li><b>1851</b>, H. Mayhew, <i>London labour and the London poor</i>, II. 150/2
<dl><dd>The sewer-hunters <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> formerly, and indeed are still, called by the name of Toshers, the articles which they pick up in the course of their wanderings along shore being known among themselves by the general term ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>’, a word more particularly applied by them to anything made of copper.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Valuables retrieved from sewers and drains
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, J. <a href = vnd.unilang:aiken.html>Aiken</a>, <i>Midnight <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Place</i>, v. 164
<dl><dd>I am present engaged in fishing for <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> in the sewers of Blastburn.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Rubbish, trash, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> especially in the sense of nonsense, bosh, balderdash
<ul><li><b>1892 October 26</b>, <i>Oxford University Magazine</i>, 26/1
<dl><dd>To think what I've <a href = vnd.unilang:gone.html>gone</a> through to hear that <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>! Frightful <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> it'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> be, too.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1911</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/H._G._Wells" class="extiw" title="w:H. G. Wells">H. G. Wells</a>, <i>The New <a href = vnd.unilang:machiavelli.html>Machiavelli</a></i>, ch. 5,
<dl><dd>Perhaps it helped a <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> into Parliament, Parliament still being a confused retrogressive corner in the world where lawyers and suchlike sheltered themselves from the onslaughts of common-sense behind a fog of Latin and Greek and twaddle and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1997</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J.K._Rowling" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J.K. Rowling">J.K. Rowling</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Harry Potter and the Philosopher | s Stone"><a href = vnd.unilang:harry.html>Harry</a> Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, iv
<dl><dd>‘<a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>Took</a> yeh from the ruined house myself, on Dumbledore’s <a href = vnd.unilang:orders.html>orders</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:brought.html>Brought</a> yeh <a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> this lot...’</dd>
<dd>‘Load of old <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>,’ <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> Uncle Vernon.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic  school <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bath or foot pan
<ul><li><b>1881</b>, Leathes in C.E. Pascoe, <i>Everyday Life in our Public Schools</i>, ii. 20
<dl><dd>A ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>’ pan... <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also provided.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1905</b>, H. A. Vachell, <i>Hill</i>, i
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> call a tub a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cricket<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Easy bowling
<ul><li><b>1898 June 25</b>, <i>Tit-Bits</i>, 252/3
<dl><dd>Among the recent neologisms of the cricket field <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> ‘<b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>’, which means bowling of contemptible easiness.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>Used as a form of address</i>.
<ul><li><b>1954</b>, E. Hyams, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>Stories</a> amp; Cream</i>, 175
<dl><dd>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ere.html>Ere</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>, you bin at <a href = vnd.unilang:cha.html>Cha</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a>?</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>See Thesaurus:nonsense</li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To steal copper, particularly from ship hulls
<ul><li><b>1867</b>, W. H. Smyth, <i>Sailor's Word-book</i></li>
<li><i><b>Toshing</b></i>, a cant word for stealing copper sheathing from vessels' <a href = vnd.unilang:bottoms.html>bottoms</a>, or from dock-yard stores.</li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To search for valuables in sewers
<ul><li><b>1974</b>, J. <a href = vnd.unilang:aiken.html>Aiken</a>, <i>Midnight <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> Place</i>, vi. 180
<dl><dd>You tend to the <b>toshing</b>, let Mester Hobday tend to the dealing.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic  school <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To use a tosh-pan, either to wash, to splash, or to "bath"
<ul><li><b>1883</b>, J.P. <a href = vnd.unilang:groves.html>Groves</a>, <i>From Cadet to <a href = vnd.unilang:captain.html>Captain</a></i>, iii. 227
<dl><dd>‘<b>Toshing</b>’ <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the name given to a punishment inflicted by the cadets on any one of their number who made himself obnoxious. The victim, dressed in full <a href = vnd.unilang:uniform.html>uniform</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> forced to run the gauntlet of his brother cadets, who, as he passed, emptied the contents of their ‘tosh-cans’ (small baths holding about three <a href = vnd.unilang:gallons.html>gallons</a> of water) <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> the wretched lad's head.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1903</b>, J. S. Farmer amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>., <i><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a></i>, VII. 171/1
<dl><dd>He <b>toshed</b> his house beak by mistake, and got three hundred.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tonce</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shorn, clipped</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tonsure</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">tosher</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">toshest</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Tight.
<ul><li><b>1776</b>, D. Herd, <i>Ancient amp; Modern Scottish <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a></i>
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>Tosh</a></b></i>, tight, neat.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Neat, clean; tidy, trim.
<ul><li><b>1794</b>, J. Ritson, <i>Scottish <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a></i>, I. 99
<dl><dd>I <a href = vnd.unilang:gang.html>gang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ay.html>ay</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fou.html>fou</a> clean and <a href = vnd.unilang:fou.html>fou</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b></dd>
<dd>As a' the neighbours can tell.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Comfortable, agreeable; friendly, intimate.
<ul><li><b>1821</b>, <i>Blackwood's Edinburgh Magazine</i>, 10 4
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a very <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> and agreeable company.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Toshly: neatly, tidily
<ul><li><b>1808</b>, J. Mayne, <i>Siller Gun</i>, i. 20
<dl><dd>Shouther your arms!—O! <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> them <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> on, And not athraw!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">toshed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To make ‘<a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a>’: to tidy, to trim.
<ul><li><b>1826 November</b>, J. Wilson, <i>Noctes Ambrosianae</i>, xxix, in <i>Blackwood's Edinburgh Magazine</i>, 788
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:hoo.html>Hoo</a> she wad try to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a> up</b>... her breest.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From 19th-century British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tosheroon</i>, from or alongside <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tusheroon</i>, of uncertain derivation from British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">caroon</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crown, a 5-shilling silver coin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mediterranean_Lingua_Franca" class="extiw" title="w:Mediterranean Lingua Franca">Sabir</a></span> and (originally) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">corona</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">crown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The term <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> either derived from or influenced by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">madza caroon</i>, the British <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> for the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mediterranean_Lingua_Franca" class="extiw" title="w:Mediterranean Lingua Franca">Sabir</a></span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:mezzo.html>mezzo</a> corona</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">half-crown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly under influence from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="Etymology_1English"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">copper <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a>; valuables</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> above or from the half-crown's value of two <a href = vnd.unilang:shillings.html>shillings</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sixpence.html>sixpence</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">toshes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A half-crown coin; its value
<ul><li><b>1933</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/George_Orwell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:George Orwell">George Orwell</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Down_and_Out_in_Paris_and_London" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Down and Out in Paris and London">Down and Out in Paris and London</a></i>, xxix
<dl><dd>‘’<a href = vnd.unilang:ere.html>Ere</a> y’are, the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> rig-out you ever ’ad. A tosheroon [<a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a crown] for the coat, two ’ogs for the trousers, one and a <a href = vnd.unilang:tanner.html>tanner</a> for the boots, and a ’<a href = vnd.unilang:og.html>og</a> for the cap and scarf. That’s seven <a href = vnd.unilang:bob.html>bob</a>.’</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1961</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:eric.html>Eric</a> Partridge,  <cite>The Routledge Dictionary of Historical <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b>tush</b> or <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b>. Money: <a href = vnd.unilang:cockney.html>Cockney</a>: late C.19–20. <a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>Ex</a>: <b>tusheroon</b>... But <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Camden_Hotten" class="extiw" title="w:John Camden Hotten">H.</a> errs, I believe: he should mean half-a-crown, for tusheroon and its C.20 variant tossaroon (2s. 6d.) are manifest corruptions of Lingua Franca MADZA CAROON.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1961</b>, J. Maclaren-Ross, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:doomsday.html>Doomsday</a> Book</i>, i. v. 63
<dl><dd>Here's a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tosh.html>tosh</a></b> to buy yourself some <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A crown coin; its value
<ul><li><b>1859</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/J.C._Hotten" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:J.C. Hotten">J.C. Hotten</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Dictionary_of_Modern_Slang,_Cant,_and_Vulgar_Words" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:A Dictionary of Modern Slang, Cant, and Vulgar Words">A Dictionary of Modern <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>Slang</a>, Cant, and Vulgar <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>Words</a></a></i>
<dl><dd><i>Half-a-crown</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> known as an <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:alderman.html>alderman</a></span>, <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a bull</span>, <span style="font-variant:small-caps;"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a> a <b>tusheroon</b></span>, and a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">madza caroon</span>; whilst a <i>crown</i> piece, or <i>five <a href = vnd.unilang:shillings.html>shillings</a></i>, may be called either a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">bull</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">caroon</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">cartwheel</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">coachwheel</span>, or a <span style="font-variant:small-caps;">thick-un</span>, or a <b><span style="font-variant:small-caps;">tusheroon</span></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1912</b>, J.W. Horsley, <i>I Remember</i>, xii. 253
<dl><dd>‘<b>Tush</b>’, for money, would be an abbreviation of ‘tusheroon’, which in old cant, and also in tinker dialect, signified a crown.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic  <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any money, particularly pre-decimalization British coinage</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a> (32233)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:toast.html>toast</a></i>. First attested in the late 1950s.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tosti.html>tosti</a>'s</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A toasted sandwich containing cheese, usually <a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a> and optionally other ingredients and condiments; a toastie.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> (117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tōte</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">tote</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">toti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to, until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toe.html>toe</a></i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">tōte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to, until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">until</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">zuo <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a></i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">total</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tōtālis</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tōtus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all, whole, entire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of unknown origin. Perhaps related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oscan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Oscan language">Oscan</a></span> <i class="Ital mention" lang="osc">𐌕𐌏𐌖𐌕𐌏</i> <span annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xum-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">totam</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tribe</span><span <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> (98597)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Emotionally moved (by), made to feel emotion (by).
<ul><li><b>1845</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Benjamin_Disraeli" class="extiw" title="w:Benjamin Disraeli">Benjamin Disraeli</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Sybil/Book_4/Chapter_1" class="extiw" title="s:Sybil/Book 4/Chapter 1">Sybil</a></i>, Book 4, Chapter 1,
<dl><dd>"They say her Majesty <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> about these affairs of the Chartists than anything else," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a> Egerton.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1868</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Louisa_May_Alcott" class="extiw" title="w:Louisa May Alcott">Louisa May Alcott</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Little_Women/Chapter_42" class="extiw" title="s:Little Women/Chapter 42">Little Women</a></i>, Part 2, Chapter 42: All Alone,
<dl><dd>“If there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> anything good or true in what I write, it isn’<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> mine. I owe it all to you and Mother and <a href = vnd.unilang:beth.html>Beth</a>,” <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jo.html>Jo</a>, more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> by her father’s <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> than by any amount of praise from the world.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1883</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jules_Verne" class="extiw" title="w:Jules Verne"><a href = vnd.unilang:jules.html>Jules</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verne.html>Verne</a></a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Hauteville (translator), <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Green_Ray/Chapter_XXI" class="extiw" title="s:The Green Ray/Chapter XXI">The Green <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>Ray</a></a></i>, Chapter XXI: A Tempest in a Cavern,
<dl><dd>“And you <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to save <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a>,” answered Miss Campbell, more <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> by the courage of the young <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> than the dangers which could still happen.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Slightly mentally deficient; <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a> in the head.
<ul><li><b>1913</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fyodor_Dostoevsky" class="extiw" title="w:Fyodor Dostoevsky">Fyodor Dostoevsky</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:eva.html>Eva</a> M. Martin (translator), <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Idiot/Part_III/Chapter_IV" class="extiw" title="s:The Idiot/Part III/Chapter IV">The Idiot</a></i>, Part III, Chapter IV,
<dl><dd>"Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you see he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a lunatic, prince?" whispered Evgenie Pavlovitch in his ear. "Someone <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> just now that he <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a bit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b> on the subject of lawyers, that he <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a mania for making <a href = vnd.unilang:speeches.html>speeches</a> and intends to pass the examinations. I am expecting a splendid burlesque now."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1922</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Joyce" class="extiw" title="w:James Joyce">James Joyce</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Ulysses_(novel)/Chapter_8" class="extiw" title="s:Ulysses (novel)/Chapter 8">Ulysses</a></i>, Episode 8: The Lestrygonians,
<dl><dd>All a bit <b><a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></b>. Mad <a href = vnd.unilang:fanny.html>Fanny</a> and his other sister <a href = vnd.unilang:mrs.html>Mrs</a> Dickinson driving about with scarlet harness.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">moved</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">affected</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">emotional</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">moved</span></li>

***toujours.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a> (87225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">tousjours</i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">toz jorz</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">tuzjurz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without ceasing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">all days</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tous</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">jours</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:altijd.html>altijd</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">altid</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>). Replaced Old French <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">sempres</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">always</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:semper.html>semper</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>always</li>
<li>still</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The "s" at the end of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a></i> will <b>not</b> trigger liaison. For example, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:toujours.html>toujours</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ici.html>ici</a></i> will be pronounced as <span class="IPA">[tu.ʒu.ʁ‿i.si]</span>.</li></ul>
</body>
